Duration: 25 mins and 37 secs
Commit: ec795aa (master)
Author: Gabriel Scherer
Message: ppx_deriving_yojson.3.3 (#13150)

(3.2 broke backward-compatibility so it was not released)

3.3
---

  * Make `_exn` functions opt-in (`[@@deriving yojson { exn = true }]`)
    to preserve backward-compatibility for fully-manual implementations
    of the [@@deriving yojson] interface.
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/86)
    Gabriel Scherer

3.2
---

  * Add `let _ = to_yojson / of_yojson` to generated code to avoid warnings when
    they aren't used
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/68)
    Steve Bleazard
  * Fix bug where doing [@@deriving of_yojson] causes an unused rec warning
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/68)
    Steve Bleazard
  * Add generated `ty_of_yojson_exn` to raise an exception rather than return an
    error
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/57, https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/68)
    Steve Bleazard
  * Port `ppx_deriving_yojson` to `dune`
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/69, https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/85)
    Rudi Grinberg, Antonio Nuno Monteiro
  * Added deriver option `fields` to generate a `Yojson_meta` module containing
    all JSON key names.
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/70)
    Steve Bleazard
  * Remove cppo that included support for versions no longer supported by
    `ppx_deriving_yojson`
    (https://github.com/ocaml-ppx/ppx_deriving_yojson/pull/75)
    Rudi Grinberg
